msg:I rarely want to review a hotel so actively, and I was really surprised. It was really a good experience at the same price, which made this hurried trip more comfortable. The hotel is excellent in many aspects, including location, service, environment, hygiene, etc., which are all good. Overall, it exceeded expectations.
The advantages of the hotel are that in addition to better service and environment, it is also very textured and detailed. There are exclusive areas in the hotel for guests, and the privacy is OK. The hotel's facilities and color matching are not bad, simple and a**ospheric, and more textured than the pictures. The opening time is not short, but the traces of use are not very obvious. At the same time, the hotel is really detailed. Although many facilities have been improved, they are more restored to the style of the Republic of China. Many details have been restored and improved, and the spare bedding even feels a bit classical (by the way, the small fresh flower arrangement on the washstand is really detailed). The overall feeling is that the scale of restoration is good, and the overall aesthetics of the hotel is advanced. The breakfast is also OK, and the taste is slightly Chinese.
There are still some disadvantages, such as the problems that may occur after many protected buildings are converted into hotels, mainly dim lighting and limited plugs (the hotel's sound insulation feels OK, which is quite unexpected). For me, the more obvious feeling is that the hotel air conditioning noise is a bit loud and there is no desk (it is not convenient to read or use a laptop).
The lady at the front desk is also very nice and took the initiative to help upgrade the room type. I highly recommend friends who like the retro style of the Republic of China to experience it. It is more interesting, but the overall environment is relatively quiet and low-key. Friends who like bustling or convenient and efficient may not feel suitable. In short, I am quite satisfied with the overall situation and can give a high score.
